# Entropy III Multiplayer Terran Scripts
# Courtesy of Broodwarai.com
# To be used with the BWAI Launcher
#=========================
#Script IDs-- For quick search just search for #scriptid; 
#searching for #aclt would take you to the Accel Terran section
#=========================
#aclt: Accel Terran (Equalizer)
#asht: Ashara Terran
#esyt: Easychat Terran
#mykt: Myk Terran
#ract: Racine Terran
#roct: Rocky Terran
#rayt: Raynor Terran
#unlt: Unleaded Terran
#warh: WarHammer Terran (Derqua)
#zldt: Zelduck Terran


# stat_txt.tbl entry 1342: Terran Expansion Custom Level<0>
TMCx(1342, 101, aiscript):
	start_town()
	transports_off()
	farms_notiming()
	groundmap_jump(begin)
	random_jump(128, roct:null)
	goto(unlt:null)



		--begin--
	enemyowns_jump(nexus, tvp)
	#TvZ and TvT
	random_jump(28, warh:null)
	random_jump(32, aclt:null)
	random_jump(36, asht:null) 
	random_jump(42, mykt:null)
	random_jump(50, ract:null)
	random_jump(64, roct:null)
	random_jump(84, rayt:null)
	random_jump(128, unlt:null)

	goto(zldt:null)
	
			--tvp--
	#For Dedicated TvP scripts, such as Easychat
	random_jump(24, warh:null)
	random_jump(28, aclt:null)
	random_jump(32, asht:null)
	random_jump(36, esyt:null)
	random_jump(42, mykt:null)
	random_jump(50, ract:null)
	random_jump(64, roct:null)
	random_jump(84, rayt:null)
	random_jump(128, unlt:null)
	goto(zldt:null)

aclt(0, 101, aiscript):
	start_town()
	farms_notiming()



	#debug(null, AccelDefault T v1.1x by Equalizer)
	--null--
#endif

	farms_notiming()
	defaultbuild_off()
	groundmap_jump(groundMap)
	#[incomplete]goto(airMap)
	stop()

	--groundMap--
	transports_off()

	build(1, Terran Command Center, 150)
	wait_buildstart(1, Terran Command Center)
	build(4, Terran SCV, 130)
	wait_buildstart(4, Terran SCV)

	define_max(8, Terran SCV)
	multirun(buildTerran SCVs)

	#Gear-up for counter zerg

	multirun(forcedExpand)
	multirun(addonControl)

	multirun(techControl)

	multirun(engineeringUpgrade2)
	multirun(armoryUpgrades)
	multirun(attackControl)

	multirun(overloadControl)
	multirun(dropshipControl)

	--requeneSupply1--
	enemyowns_jump(Protoss Gateway, counterRush)
	enemyowns_jump(Zerg Spawning Pool, counterRush)

	resources_jump(140, 0, accelerateSupply1) 
	wait(50)
	goto(requeneSupply1)
	--accelerateSupply1--
	build(1, Terran Supply Depot, 80)
	wait_buildstart(1, Terran Supply Depot)

	enemyowns_jump(Protoss Gateway, counterRush)
	enemyowns_jump(Zerg Spawning Pool, counterRush)

	enemyowns_jump(Zerg Spawning Pool, counterRush)

	wait_buildstart(2, Terran Supply Depot)

	define_max(17, Terran SCV)

	wait(50)

	define_max(12, Terran Marine)

# =====Cheese=====

#- TvZ Misc

unlt(0, 101, aiscript):
	start_town()
	transports_off()
	farms_notiming()



	#debug(null, Unleaded Terran 3.06 by Archon_Wing)
	--null--
#endif
	defaultbuild_off()
	define_max(58, marine)
	define_max(70, scv)
	define_max(12, medic)
	define_max(20, siege_tank)
	define_max(20, goliath)
	define_max(255, wraith)
	define_max(2, dropship)
	define_max(20, battlecruiser)
	define_max(10, science_vessel)
	define_max(3, ghost)
	define_max(1, nuclear_missile)
	define_max(8, firebat)
	define_max(20, vulture)
	build(1, command_center, 150)
	wait_build(1, command_center)
	build(7, scv, 80)
	multirun(comsat)
	multirun(cloak_detect)
	wait_buildstart(7, scv)
	multirun(essentials)
	groundmap_jump(block1)

	goto(island)
			--block1--
# Don't ever BBS if enemy is rushing

	random_jump(5, bbs)
	--do stuff--

	race_jump(tvt, tvz, tvp)
# =====Cheese=====
#Proxy Raxes
			--bbs--
	enemyresources_jump(100, 0, do stuff)
	rush(0, do stuff)
	random_jump(140, bbs 2)
	enemyowns_jump(nexus, tvp)
	#don't bbs protoss as much	
		--bbs 2--
	define_max(9, scv)
	wait(450)
	expand(1, blank)
	expand(2, proxy)

	multirun(force rax)
	--wait rax--
	wait(25)
	notowns_jump(barracks, wait rax)
	build(1, supply_depot, 80)
	player_need(1, barracks)
	multirun(bbs attack)
	train(6, marine)
	farms_timing()
	attack_add(5, marine)
	define_max(70, scv)
	multirun(scv)
	attack_do()
	attack_clear()
	defenseuse_gg(1, marine)
	defenseuse_aa(1, marine)
	defenseuse_ag(1, marine)
	defenseuse_ga(1, marine)
	train(6, marine)
	attack_add(7, marine)
	attack_do()
	attack_clear()
	clear_combatdata()
	build(1, refinery, 95)
	wait_buildstart(1, refinery)
	race_jump(tvt, tvz follow up, tvp)
	
	--tvz follow up--
	player_need(2, barracks)

	multirun(ebay_up)
